 No one can deny that a child cannot understand as much as his parents understand
 ek bachche ke liye kya sahi he or kya galat
 
 
 Hardly anyone can decide this better than parents
 vahiin duusari ore lagbhag har bachche ke liye uske mummy-papa hi pehle role model hote hai
 Even the smallest habits of parents have a profound effect on children
 psychology kii imitesan theory se ye sabit bhi hota he kibache saamaajik vyavhaaypane mata-pita se hi sikhte hai
 By the way, it is the best effort of parents not to do anything that has a bad effect on the child, but sometimes such mistakes happen and the children make them part of their behavior
 aise main ye aadaten unke liye nuksaandeh sabit ho sakati hai
 These are the 7 things that every parent should take care of
 
 
 1
 Sometimes we start criticizing ourselves for our looks and career
 aisa karne se bachche ke man main sundarataa or safalataa ko lekar negative baaten ghar kar sakati hai
 Due to which he may complain of depression and irritability later on
 2
 Many parents are on the phone for hours
 unhen dekhakar unke bachein bhi bahut kam umr main hi mobile kii maang karne lagate hai
 This may affect their studies
 3
 Many parents have this habit that they ask their children to behave according to whether they are boys or girls
 jaise agar ladki he to unhen yah naseehat di jaati he ki wo sports main bhaag naa len or ladakon ko apni bhaawanaaon ko chhipaane kii salaah di jaati he
 Doing so has negative effects on children
 4
 Never smoke nor drink alcohol in front of children
 bacchon ke saamne aisa karne se unhen lag saktaa he ki dhumrapaan karne or sharaab pine main koi buraai nahin he
 This can make them a victim of this dirty addiction at a very young age
 5
 Never compare your children to other children
 naa hi kabhi kam number laane ke liye duusare bacchon ke saamne apane bacchon ko daantnaa chahie
 Doing so can hurt your child's self-esteem
 6
 If you fight with other family members in front of your children then it can have a bad effect on them
 ho saktaa he is choti si umr main hi wo bahut aakraamak ho jaaen
 7
 choti-choti galatiyon ke liye apane bacchon par kabhi haath nahin uthaanaa chahie
 If you punish them on trivial matters, then the feeling of opposition may come in them and they may even stop honoring you

 The apex court said on Monday that it would consider whether to impose a complete ban on plastics keeping in mind the interests of cattle and the environment
 nyaayamurti jies singhvi or nyaayamurti esaje mukhopadhyaay kii peeth ne ek janhit yachika par sunwaayee ke dauraan yah baat kahi
 The petition drew the court's attention to the condition of the animals, who are also allegedly swallowing plastic along with their food
 yachika karunaa socity for animal and nechar ne daayar kii he
 Hearing the petition, the court issued notices to the central and state governments and the plastic manufacturers
 nyaayalay ne suzav diya ki yaa to plastic ke istemaal par purna pratibandh hona chahie yaa nirmaataaon ko istemaal kiye gaye plastic ko chunakar uskaa punarchakran karnaa chahie
 The petition demanded that the court direct the government to ban the use, sale of plastic bags in all municipalities and municipal corporations and end the 'open garbage disposal system' in a phased manner
 tippaniyan The ngo's petition also demanded issuing instructions for municipalities and municipal corporations to collect garbage at every door
 yachika main maang kii gai ki nagar palika nikaay yah tay kare ki kooda gharon kaa nirmaan or prabandhan aisa ho ki uske aasapaas pashu nahin aa saken
 a bench of Justice GS Singhvi and Justice SJ Mukhopadhyay stated this while hearing a PIL
 yachika main pashuon kii sthiti par nyaayalay kaa dhyaan aakarshith kiya gaya he, jo kathith rup se apane bhojan ke saath plastic bhi nigal rahe hai
 The petition has been filed by the Karuna Society for Animals and Nature
 yachika par sunwaayee karte hue nyaayalay ne centre evam rajya sarkaron or plastic nirmaataaon ko notice jari kiye
 The court suggested that there should either be a complete ban on the use of plastics or that manufacturers should choose and recycle the used plastics
